   <script>
    /**
 * Function that tracks a click on an outbound link in Analytics.
 * This function takes a valid URL string as an argument, and uses that URL string
 * as the event label. Setting the transport method to 'beacon' lets the hit be sent
 * using 'navigator.sendBeacon' in browser that support it.
 */
 var trackOutboundLink = function(url) {
    ga('send', 'event', 'outbound', 'click', url, {
      'transport': 'beacon',
      'hitCallback': function(){document.location = url;}
    });
 }
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function UpdateLink(link)
 		{
 			link.href = link.name + document.body.scrollTop.toString();
 		}
 
 function MM_swapImgRestore() { //v3.0
   var i,x,a=document.MM_sr; for(i=0;a&&i<a.length&&(x=a[i])&&x.oSrc;i++) x.src=x.oSrc;
 }
 
 function MM_preloadImages() { //v3.0
   var d=document; if(d.images){ if(!d.MM_p) d.MM_p=new Array();
     var i,j=d.MM_p.length,a=MM_preloadImages.arguments; for(i=0; i<a.length; i++)
     if (a[i].indexOf("#")!=0){ d.MM_p[j]=new Image; d.MM_p[j++].src=a[i];}}
 }
 
 function MM_findObj(n, d) { //v4.0
   var p,i,x;  if(!d) d=document; if((p=n.indexOf("?"))>0&&parent.frames.length) {
     d=parent.frames[n.substring(p+1)].document; n=n.substring(0,p);}
   if(!(x=d[n])&&d.all) x=d.all[n]; for (i=0;!x&&i<d.forms.length;i++) x=d.forms[i][n];
   for(i=0;!x&&d.layers&&i<d.layers.length;i++) x=MM_findObj(n,d.layers[i].document);
   if(!x && document.getElementById) x=document.getElementById(n); return x;
 }
 
 function MM_swapImage() { //v3.0
   var i,j=0,x,a=MM_swapImage.arguments; document.MM_sr=new Array; for(i=0;i<(a.length-2);i+=3)
    if ((x=MM_findObj(a[i]))!=null){document.MM_sr[j++]=x; if(!x.oSrc) x.oSrc=x.src; x.src=a[i+2];}
 }
 
 function OpenWindow(link,WindowName)
 {
 window.open(link,WindowName,'toolbar=0,location=0,directories=0,status=0,menubar=0,scrollbars=1,resizable=1,width=620,height=580');
 }
   </script>

   <!-- CC Car model search - improved by Satish-Webplanex 9/8/2017 -->
   <script src="js/jquery.uniform.js" type="text/javascript">
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
 	
 	  $(function(){
 	    $("select").uniform(); 
 	  });
 		myajax_func_cmbmake('#cmbmake','make','','','');
 
 		$(document).on('change','#cmbmake',function(){
 			if($(this).val() != ''){
 				myajax_func_cmbmake('#cmbmodel','model',$('#cmbmake').val(),'','');
 			}else{
 				$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('');
 				$('#cmbmodel').html('<option value="">Model</option>');
 				$('#cmbbodystyle').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 				$.uniform.update('#cmbmodel');
 				$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle');
 			}
 		});
 		$(document).on('change','#cmbmodel',function(){
 			if($(this).val() != ''){
 				myajax_func_cmbmake('#cmbbodystyle','bdstyle',$('#cmbmake').val(),$('#cmbmodel').val(),'');
 			}else{
 					$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('');
 					$('#cmbbodystyle').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle');
 			}
 		});
 		$(document).on('change','#cmbbodystyle',function(){
 			if($(this).val() != ''){
 				myajax_func_cmbmake('','cuft1115',$('#cmbmake').val(),$('#cmbmodel').val(),$(this).val());
 			}else{
 					$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('');
 			}
 		});
 	});
 function myajax_func_cmbmake(objid, str, mymakeparam,mymodelparam,cuft1115){ 
 	$.ajax({
 			type: 'POST',
 			url: 'ajax_request.asp',
 			data: {strtype : str, mymakeparam : mymakeparam, mymodelparam : mymodelparam, cuft1115 : cuft1115},
 			success: function(resdata){
 				console.log(resdata);
 				if(resdata == "1" || resdata == "2" || resdata == "3" || resdata == "4"){
 					if(str == "bdstyle"){
 						$('#cmbbodystyle').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 						$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle');
 						$('#uniform-cmbbodystyle').hide();
 					}
 					if(resdata == "1")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('11 cu. ft. or 15 cu. ft.');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake").show();
 					if(resdata == "2")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('11 cu. ft.');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake").show();
 					if(resdata == "3")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('15 cu. ft.');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake").show();
 					if(resdata == "4")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('Not recommended for your car');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake").show();
 				}
 				else{
 					$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake .fitting-head-cmbmake").html('');
 					if(str == "bdstyle"){
 						$('#uniform-cmbbodystyle').show();
 					}
 					else{
 						$('#uniform-cmbbodystyle').hide();
 					}
 					$(objid).html(resdata);
 					if(str == 'make'){
 						$('#cmbmodel').html('<option value="">Model</option>');
 						$('#cmbbodystyle').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 					}
 					if(str == 'model'){
 						$('#cmbbodystyle').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');				
 					}
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbmake');
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbmodel');
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle');
 				}
 			},
 			error: function(){
 					
 			}
 		});
 }
   </script>

 				myajax_func_cmbmake2('#cmbmodel2','model',$('#cmbmake2').val(),'','');
 			}else{
 				$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('');
 				$('#cmbmodel2').html('<option value="">Model</option>');
 				$('#cmbbodystyle2').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 				$.uniform.update('#cmbmodel2');
 				$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle2');
 			}
 		});
 		$(document).on('change','#cmbmodel2',function(){
 			if($(this).val() != ''){
 				myajax_func_cmbmake2('#cmbbodystyle2','bdstyle',$('#cmbmake2').val(),$('#cmbmodel2').val(),'');
 			}else{
 					$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('');
 					$('#cmbbodystyle2').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle2');
 			}
 		});
 		$(document).on('change','#cmbbodystyle2',function(){
 			if($(this).val() != ''){
 				myajax_func_cmbmake2('','cuft1115',$('#cmbmake2').val(),$('#cmbmodel2').val(),$(this).val());
 			}else{
 					$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('');
 			}
 		});
 	});
 function myajax_func_cmbmake2(objid, str, mymakeparam,mymodelparam,cuft1115){ 
 	$.ajax({
 			type: 'POST',
 			url: 'ajax_request.asp',
 			data: {strtype : str, mymakeparam : mymakeparam, mymodelparam : mymodelparam, cuft1115 : cuft1115},
 			success: function(resdata){
 				if(resdata == "1" || resdata == "2" || resdata == "3" || resdata == "4"){
 					if(str == "bdstyle"){
 						$('#cmbbodystyle2').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 						$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle2');
 						$('#uniform-cmbbodystyle2').hide();
 					}
 					if(resdata == "1")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('11 cu. ft. or 15 cu. ft.');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2").show();
 					if(resdata == "2")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('11 cu. ft.');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2").show();
 					if(resdata == "3")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('15 cu. ft.');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2").show();
 					if(resdata == "4")
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('Not recommended for your car');
 						$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2").show();
 				}
 				else{
 					$(".suggested-wrap-cmbmake2 .fitting-head-cmbmake2").html('');
 					if(str == "bdstyle"){
 						$('#uniform-cmbbodystyle2').show();
 					}
 					else{
 						$('#uniform-cmbbodystyle2').hide();
 					}
 					$(objid).html(resdata);
 					if(str == 'make'){
 						$('#cmbmodel2').html('<option value="">Model</option>');
 						$('#cmbbodystyle2').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');
 					}
 					if(str == 'model'){
 						$('#cmbbodystyle2').html('<option value="">Body Style</option>');				
 					}
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbmake2');
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbmodel2');
 					$.uniform.update('#cmbbodystyle2');
 				}
 			},
 			error: function(){
 					
 			}
 		});
 }
   </script>

   <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    function showHide(shID) {
    if (document.getElementById(shID)) {
       if (document.getElementById(shID+'-show').style.display != 'none') {
          document.getElementById(shID+'-show').style.display = 'none';
          document.getElementById(shID).style.display = 'block';
       }
       else {
          document.getElementById(shID+'-show').style.display = 'inline';
          document.getElementById(shID).style.display = 'none';
       }
    }
 }
   </script>

 /*Code created by Komal to store selected value from user when they back from product page*/
 
 function scrollToElement(ele) {
     //$(window).scrollTop(ele.offset().top).scrollLeft(ele.offset().left);
     $(window).load(function(){
         $(window).scrollTop(ele.offset().top).scrollLeft(ele.offset().left);
     });
     
 }//This function is created to let user land directly to the EX section when they come back from detail page.
 
 $(document).ready(function(){
 
     $("#ClickForDimensions").click(function(e){
         e.preventDefault();//this will prevent the link trying to navigate to another page
         var href = $(this).attr("href");//get the href so we can navigate later
         //do the update
         localStorage.setItem("link","CC");
         //when update has finished, navigate to the other page
         window.location = href;
     });
 
     $("#ClickForDimensionsEx").click(function(e){
         e.preventDefault();//this will prevent the link trying to navigate to another page
         var href = $(this).attr("href");//get the href so we can navigate later
         //do the update
         localStorage.setItem("link","EX");
         //when update has finished, navigate to the other page
         window.location = href;
     });
     
     if (localStorage.getItem("link") !== null && localStorage.getItem("link")=="CC"){
         scrollToElement($('#CC'));
     }
     else if(localStorage.getItem("link") !== null && localStorage.getItem("link")=="EX"){
         scrollToElement($('#EX'));
     }
 
 if (localStorage.getItem("product_type") !== null) {
 	if(localStorage.getItem("product_type")=="CC")
 	{
 		if(localStorage.getItem("straps") !== null && localStorage.getItem("straps")=="rack")
 		{
 			$(".CC-straps:nth(0)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".CC-straps:nth(0)").trigger('change');
 
 		}
 		else if(localStorage.getItem("straps") !== null && localStorage.getItem("straps")=="no_rack")
 		{
 			$(".CC-straps:nth(1)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".CC-straps:nth(1)").trigger('change');
 		}
                 if(localStorage.getItem("color") !== null && localStorage.getItem("color")=="bk")
 		{
 			$(".CC-color:nth(0)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".CC-color:nth(0)").trigger('change');
 
 		}
 		else if(localStorage.getItem("color") !== null && localStorage.getItem("color")=="gy")
 		{
 			$(".CC-color:nth(1)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".CC-color:nth(1)").trigger('change');
 		}
                 if(localStorage.getItem("size") !== null && localStorage.getItem("size")=="11")
 		{
 			$(".CC-size:nth(0)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".CC-size:nth(0)").trigger('change');
 
 		}
 		else if(localStorage.getItem("size") !== null && localStorage.getItem("size")=="15")
 		{
 			$(".CC-size:nth(1)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".CC-size:nth(1)").trigger('change');
 		}
 	}
 	else if(localStorage.getItem("product_type")=="EX")
 	{
 		if(localStorage.getItem("straps") !== null && localStorage.getItem("straps")=="rack")
 		{
 			$(".EX-straps:nth(0)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".EX-straps:nth(0)").trigger('change');
 		}
 		else if(localStorage.getItem("straps") !== null && localStorage.getItem("straps")=="no_rack")
 		{
 			$(".EX-straps:nth(1)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".EX-straps:nth(1)").trigger('change');
 		}
                 if(localStorage.getItem("color") !== null && localStorage.getItem("color")=="bk")
 		{
 			$(".EX-color:nth(0)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".EX-color:nth(0)").trigger('change');
 
 		}
 		else if(localStorage.getItem("color") !== null && localStorage.getItem("color")=="gy")
 		{
 			$(".EX-color:nth(1)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".EX-color:nth(1)").trigger('change');
 		}
                 if(localStorage.getItem("size") !== null && localStorage.getItem("size")=="11")
 		{
 			$(".EX-size:nth(0)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".EX-size:nth(0)").trigger('change');
 
 		}
 		else if(localStorage.getItem("size") !== null && localStorage.getItem("size")=="15")
 		{
 			$(".EX-size:nth(1)").prop('checked', 'checked');
                         $(".EX-size:nth(1)").trigger('change');
 		}
 	}
 }
 });
 
 /*Local Storage code completed*/
 
 
 /*Function to Change image created by Komal*/
 function changeImg(style)
 {
         if(style=='CC')
         {
             /*Image changes for CC Car Top Carrier*/
             var cc_straps = (!$(".CC-straps:nth(0)").is(':checked'))?(!$(".CC-straps:nth(1)").is(':checked'))?'':($(".CC-straps:nth(1)").val()):($(".CC-straps:nth(0)").val());
             var cc_color = (!$(".CC-color:nth(0)").is(':checked'))?(!$(".CC-color:nth(1)").is(':checked'))?'':($(".CC-color:nth(1)").val()):($(".CC-color:nth(0)").val());
             var cc_size = (!$(".CC-size:nth(0)").is(':checked'))?(!$(".CC-size:nth(1)").is(':checked'))?'':($(".CC-size:nth(1)").val()):($(".CC-size:nth(0)").val());
             /*Set values in local storage for further use*/
             if(localStorage.getItem("product_type")=="EX"){
                 localStorage.removeItem("straps");
                 localStorage.removeItem("color");
                 localStorage.removeItem("size");
             }
             localStorage.setItem("product_type","CC");
 
             if(cc_straps=='rack') /*Only Rack*/
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("straps","rack");
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack')/*Only No Rack*/
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("straps","no_rack");
             }
             if(cc_color=='bk')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("color","bk");
             }
             else if(cc_color=='gy')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("color","gy");
             }
             if(cc_size =='11')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("size","11");
             }
             else if(cc_size =='15')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("size","15");
             }
             /*Set values in local storage for further use*/
 
             /*Gallery Small and big image changes Start*/
             if(cc_straps=='rack') /*Only Rack*/
             {				
                 $('#alt_image_0').attr('src','Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackCC50BK.jpg');
                 $('#alt_image_1').attr('src','Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackCC50GY.jpg');
                 fetchImage("alt_image_0", "Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackCC240BK.jpg" );
                 fetchImage("alt_image_1", "Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackCC240GY.jpg");
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack')/*Only No Rack*/
             {
                 $('#alt_image_0').attr('src','Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackCC50BK.jpg');
                 $('#alt_image_1').attr('src','Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackCC50GY.jpg');
                 fetchImage("alt_image_0", "Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackCC240BK.jpg" );
                 fetchImage("alt_image_1", "Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackCC240GY.jpg" );
             }
             /*Gallery Small and big image changes End*/
 
             if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='' && cc_size =='') /*Only Rack*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='' && cc_size =='')/*Only No Rack*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='bk' && cc_size =='')/*Rack and Black*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='gy' && cc_size =='')/*Rack and Gray*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='bk' && cc_size =='')/*No Rack and Black*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');                    
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='gy' && cc_size =='')/*No Rack and Gray*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='bk' && cc_size =='11')/*Rack, Black and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='gy' && cc_size =='11')/*Rack, Gray and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-11.jpg');                    
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='bk' && cc_size =='11')/*No Rack, Black and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='gy' && cc_size =='11')/*No Rack, Gray and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='bk' && cc_size =='15')/*Rack, Black and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-15.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='rack' && cc_color=='gy' && cc_size =='15')/*Rack, Gray and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-15.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='bk' && cc_size =='15')/*No Rack, Black and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-15.jpg');
             }
             else if(cc_straps=='no_rack' && cc_color=='gy' && cc_size =='15')/*No Rack, Gray and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier -Gy-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage2').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-CC-Car-Top-Carrier -Gy-15.jpg');
             }
             /*Image changes for CC Car Top Carrier*/
 
             /*Link changes for CC Car Top Carrier*/
                 changeLink(style,cc_straps,cc_color);
             /*Link changes for CC Car Top Carrier*/
         }
 
         else if(style='EX')
         {
             /*Image changes for EX Car Top Carrier*/
             var ex_straps = (!$(".EX-straps:nth(0)").is(':checked'))?(!$(".EX-straps:nth(1)").is(':checked'))?'':($(".EX-straps:nth(1)").val()):($(".EX-straps:nth(0)").val());
             var ex_color = (!$(".EX-color:nth(0)").is(':checked'))?(!$(".EX-color:nth(1)").is(':checked'))?'':($(".EX-color:nth(1)").val()):($(".EX-color:nth(0)").val());
             var ex_size = (!$(".EX-size:nth(0)").is(':checked'))?(!$(".EX-size:nth(1)").is(':checked'))?'':($(".EX-size:nth(1)").val()):($(".EX-size:nth(0)").val());
 
             /*Set values in local storage for further use*/
             if(localStorage.getItem("product_type")=="CC"){
                 localStorage.removeItem("straps");
                 localStorage.removeItem("color");
                 localStorage.removeItem("size");
             }
             localStorage.setItem("product_type","EX");
             if(ex_straps=='rack') /*Only Rack*/
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("straps","rack");
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack')/*Only No Rack*/
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("straps","no_rack");
             }
             if(ex_color=='bk')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("color","bk");
             }
             else if(ex_color=='gy')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("color","gy");
             }
             if(ex_size =='11')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("size","11");
             }
             else if(ex_size =='15')
             {
                 localStorage.setItem("size","15");
             }
             /*Set values in local storage for further use*/
 
             /*Gallery Small and big image changes Start*/
             if(ex_straps=='rack') /*Only Rack*/
             {
                 $('#alt_image_4').attr('src','Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackExp50BK.jpg');
                 $('#alt_image_5').attr('src','Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackExp50GY.jpg');
                 fetchImage3("alt_image_4", "Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackExp240BK.jpg" );
                 fetchImage3("alt_image_5", "Images/StrapsForRack/2StrapsRackExp240GY.jpg" );
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack')/*Only No Rack*/
             {
                 $('#alt_image_4').attr('src','Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackExp50BK.jpg');
                 $('#alt_image_5').attr('src','Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackExp50GY.jpg');
                 fetchImage3("alt_image_4", "Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackExp240BK.jpg" );
                 fetchImage3("alt_image_5", "Images/StrapsForNoRack/2StrapsNoRackExp240GY.jpg" );
             }
             /*Gallery Small and big image changes End*/
 
             if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='' && ex_size =='') /*Only Rack*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='' && ex_size =='')/*Only No Rack*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='bk' && ex_size =='')/*Rack and Black*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='gy' && ex_size =='')/*Rack and Gray*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='bk' && ex_size =='')/*No Rack and Black*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='gy' && ex_size =='')/*No Rack and Gray*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='bk' && ex_size =='11')/*Rack, Black and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='gy' && ex_size =='11')/*Rack, Gray and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='bk' && ex_size =='11')/*No Rack, Black and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='gy' && ex_size =='11')/*No Rack, Gray and 11*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy-11.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy-11.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='bk' && ex_size =='15')/*Rack, Black and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Bk-15.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='rack' && ex_color=='gy' && ex_size =='15')/*Rack, Gray and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Rack-Gy-15.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='bk' && ex_size =='15')/*No Rack, Black and 15*/
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Bk-15.jpg');
             }
             else if(ex_straps=='no_rack' && ex_color=='gy' && ex_size =='15')/*No Rack, Gray and 15*/
 
             {
                     $('#prodImage3').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier-Gy-15.jpg');
                     //$('#prodImage4').attr('src','Images/Products/RoofBag-EX-Car-Top-Carrier -Gy-15.jpg');
             }
             /*Image changes for EX Car Top Carrier*/
 
             /*Link changes for EX Car Top Carrier*/
                 changeLink(style,ex_straps,ex_color);
             /*Link changes for EX Car Top Carrier*/
             }    
 }
 /*Change image function end*/
 
 /*Change link function start*/
 function changeLink(style,straps,color)
 {
     if(style=='CC')
     {
         if(straps=='rack' && (color=='' || color=='bk'))/*Only Rack or Rack and Black*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensions').attr('href','/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Black.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Black.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='rack' && color=='gy')/*CC, Rack and Gray*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensions').attr('href','/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Gray.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Gray.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='no_rack' && color=='')/*Only No Rack*/
         {
 	    $('#ClickForDimensions').attr('href','/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='no_rack' && color=='bk')/*CC, No Rack and Black*/
         {
 	    $('#ClickForDimensions').attr('href','/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='no_rack' && color=='gy')/*CC, No Rack and Gray*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensions').attr('href','/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Gray.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Cross-Country-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Gray.asp';");
         }
     }
     else if(style=='EX')
     {
         if(straps=='rack' && (color=='' || color=='bk'))/*Only Rack or Rack and Black*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensionsEx').attr('href','/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Black.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder3').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Black.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='rack' && color=='gy')/*EX, Rack and Gray*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensionsEx').attr('href','/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Gray.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder3').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-With-Rack-Gray.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='no_rack' && color=='')/*Only No Rack*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensionsEx').attr('href','/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder3').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='no_rack' && color=='bk')/*EX, No Rack and Black*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensionsEx').attr('href','/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder3').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Black.asp';");
         }
         else if(straps=='no_rack' && color=='gy')/*EX, No Rack and Gray*/
         {
             $('#ClickForDimensionsEx').attr('href','/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Gray.asp');
             $('#imagePlaceHolder3').attr("onclick","location.href='https://www.roofbag.com/Explorer-Car-Top-Carrier-Cars-Without-Rack-Gray.asp';");
         }
     }
 }
 /*Change link function end*/
   </script>
   <!------Popup Script: Do I need this? ------ #11 - PM--------->
   <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(window).ready(function() {
 			
 			/*
 			 * Resets and repositions all elements when called.
 			 */	
 			// resize explicitly
 			jQuery(window).bind('resize', function() {
 				jQuery().popup('reposition');
 			});
 			
 			/*****
 				Popup#1 - PM
 			*****/
 			jQuery('#struct11').popup({innerHTML: 'p'})
 			.popup('assign', jQuery('#handler11'), 'mouseenter', 'show', {
 				position: {
 					relativeTo: jQuery('#handler11'), 
 					x: 'right',
 					y: 'bottom',
 					z: 7000 ,
 					position: 'absolute'					
 				}, 
 				showOptions: {opacity: 1, duration: 250},
 				hideOptions: {duration: 250}
 			})
 			.popup('assign', jQuery('#handler11'), 'mouseleave', 'hide');
 			
 			jQuery('#struct11').bind({
 				'regionOver.popup': function() {
 					jQuery(this).popup('show', {opacity: 1, duration: 250});
 				},
 				'regionOut.popup': function() {
 					jQuery(this).popup('hide', {duration: 250});
 				}
 			});
 			
 		});
   </script>
   <!-- End of PM popup script -->

   <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    function showHide(shID) {
    if (document.getElementById(shID)) {
       if (document.getElementById(shID+'-show').style.display != 'none') {
          document.getElementById(shID+'-show').style.display = 'none';
          document.getElementById(shID).style.display = 'block';
       }
       else {
          document.getElementById(shID+'-show').style.display = 'inline';
          document.getElementById(shID).style.display = 'none';
       }
    }
 }
   </script>

   <script>
    (function(d, s, id) {
   var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
   if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
   js = d.createElement(s); js.id = id;
   js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js#xfbml=1&version=v2.10";
   fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
 }(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));
   </script>

   <!--
 <HTML><head>
 <link rel="stylesheet" href="styles.css" type="text/css">
 <meta http-equiv="Content-Type" content="text/html; charset=iso-8859-1">
 <META NAME="keywords" CONTENT="car top carrier, roof rack, cargo carrier,luggage roof carrier,car top cargo carrier,bars,nets,luggge,cartop,vehicle,roof,rack,organizers,car,truck,van,organized,trip,CAR,TOP,CARRIERS,ROOF,RACKS,LUGGAGE,CARGO,BARS,RACKS">

   <script language="Javascript" type="text/javascript">
    var viewerType = "0";
 
   var fetchedImages = {};
   var fetchedImages2 = {};
   var fetchedImages3 = {};
   var fetchedImages4 = {};
   var imgThumbArr = [];
   var imgThumbArr2 = [];
   var imgThumbArr3 = [];
   var imgThumbArr4 = [];  
   var zoomLevel = 0;
   var zoomFetches = {};
   var NUMZOOMLEVELS = 5;
   var zoomViewerHTML = "";
   var allPreloaded = 0;
   var numberToPreload = 8;
   var preloadCount = 0;
   var arrayindex = 0;
   var zoomimages=0;
   var tszoom=0;
 
 function viewerZoomIn()
 {
   if(viewerType == "s7") {
     tszoom.zoomIn();
   } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
     DynAPI.view.zoomIn();
   } 
   setZoomButtons();
 }
 
 function viewerZoomOut()
 {
   if(viewerType == "s7") {
     tszoom.zoomOut();
   } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
     DynAPI.view.zoomOut();
   } 
   setZoomButtons();
 }
 
 function viewerReset()
 {
   if(viewerType == "s7") {
     tszoom.reset();
   } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
     DynAPI.view.reset();
   }
   setZoomButtons(1); 
 }
 
 function viewerShowZoomImage(url, width, height, version, amzZoomViewerType, scaleLevels) 
 {
   if(viewerType == "s7") {
     tszoom.setImage(url,true,width,height);
   } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
     DynAPI.view.setZoomImage(url + ".",width,height,version,amzZoomViewerType,scaleLevels);
   }
   setZoomButtons(1); 
 }
 
 
 function zoomFetchImage(id, image)
 {
   // This method fetches the six (three on/off) buttons so that they can be 
   // changed dynamically. The image index are 0/1 -- Zoom+ : on/off, 2/3 -- Zoom- : on/off
   // 4/5 --  Reset : on/off
 
   zoomFetches[id] = {};
   zoomFetches[id].image = image;
 
   // Attempt to preload the button images
   var imagePreloader = new Image();
   imagePreloader.src = zoomFetches[id].image;
 }
 
 function setZoomButtons(reset)
 {
   if(viewerType == "s7") {
     if (tszoom.visible != 0) {
       if( document.getElementById('zoomIn') &&
           document.getElementById('zoomOut') &&
           document.getElementById('reset') ) {
 
         if (tszoom.zoomi.curZoomPower == 0 || reset) {
           document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominon"].image;
           document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomoutoff"].image;
           document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["resetoff"].image;
         } else if (tszoom.zoomi.curZoomPower >= tszoom.zoomi.max_zoom) {
           document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominoff"].image;
           document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomouton"].image;
           document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["reseton"].image;
         } else {
           document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominon"].image;
           document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomouton"].image;
           document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["reseton"].image;
         }
       }
     }
   } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
       if( document.getElementById('zoomIn') &&
           document.getElementById('zoomOut') &&
           document.getElementById('reset') ) {
 
 	var zoomLevel = DynAPI.view.getZoomLevel();
 
         if (zoomLevel == -1 || reset) {
           document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominon"].image;
           document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomoutoff"].image;
           document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["resetoff"].image;
         } else if (zoomLevel == 1) {
           document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominoff"].image;
           document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomouton"].image;
           document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["reseton"].image;
         } else {
           document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominon"].image;
           document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomouton"].image;
           document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["reseton"].image;
         }
       }      
   }
 }
 
 function zoomButtonsOff()
 {
   if( document.getElementById('zoomIn') &&
       document.getElementById('zoomOut') &&
       document.getElementById('reset') ) {
     document.getElementById('zoomIn').src  = zoomFetches["zoominoff"].image;
     document.getElementById('zoomOut').src = zoomFetches["zoomoutoff"].image;
     document.getElementById('reset').src   = zoomFetches["resetoff"].image;
   }
 }
 
 function fetchImage( id, image) 
 {
  
    fetchedImages[id] = {};
    fetchedImages[id].image = image;
    imgThumbArr[arrayindex] = id;
    arrayindex++;
 
    if(preloadCount < numberToPreload) 
    {
      var imagePreloader = new Image();
      imagePreloader.src = image;
      preloadCount++;
    }
 
 }
 
 
 
 
 
 
 function showZoomViewer()
 {
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').innerHTML = '<div width="0" height="0"></div>';
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').style.width = 0;
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').style.height = 0;
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').style.visibility = "hidden";
 
     document.getElementById('zoomTextDiv').innerHTML = ' ';
     document.getElementById('zoomButtonsDiv').innerHTML = zoomButtons;
 
     if(viewerType == "s7") {
       document.getElementById('tsapi').style.visibility = "visible";
       document.getElementById('tsapi').style.width = 240;
       document.getElementById('tsapi').style.height = 144;
 
       tszoom.setVisible(1);
       tszoom.setWidth(400);
       tszoom.setHeight(400);
     } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
       document.getElementById('zoomViewerDiv').style.visibility = "visible";
       document.getElementById('zoomViewerDiv').style.width = 240;
       document.getElementById('zoomViewerDiv').style.height = 144;
 
       DynAPI.view.show();
     }
 }
 
 
 
 
 function showImage( id )
 {
     if(viewerType == "s7") {
       if(tszoom) {
         tszoom.setVisible(0);
         tszoom.setWidth(0);
         tszoom.setHeight(0);
 
         document.getElementById('tsapi').style.visibility = "hidden";
         document.getElementById('tsapi').style.width = 0;
         document.getElementById('tsapi').style.height = 0;
 
         document.getElementById('zoomTextDiv').innerHTML = '';
         document.getElementById('zoomButtonsDiv').innerHTML = '';
       }
     } else if (viewerType == "amz") {
       if(DynAPI && DynAPI.view) {
   	DynAPI.view.hide();
 
         document.getElementById('zoomViewerDiv').style.visibility = "hidden";
         document.getElementById('zoomViewerDiv').style.width = 0;
         document.getElementById('zoomViewerDiv').style.height = 0;
 
         document.getElementById('zoomTextDiv').innerHTML = '';
         document.getElementById('zoomButtonsDiv').innerHTML = '';
       }
     }
 
     showImageViewer( id )
 }
 
 function showImageViewer( id )
 {
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').style.width = 240;
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').style.height = 144;
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').style.visibility = "visible";
 
     document.getElementById('imageViewerDiv').innerHTML = '<img src="" id="prodImage" />';
     document.getElementById('prodImage').src = fetchedImages[id].image;
 
     for ( elementID in fetchedImages )
     {
       if ( !allPreloaded )
       {
         var imagePreloader = new Image();
         imagePreloader.src = fetchedImages[elementID].image;
       }
     }
     allPreloaded = 1;
 }
 
 function setImageBorder(id) 
 {
    if(document.getElementById)
     {
 	for (var i=0; i < imgThumbArr.length; i++ )
         {
            if (document.getElementById(imgThumbArr[i]))
            {
 	     document.getElementById(imgThumbArr[i]).className = 'image';
            }
 	}
 	document.getElementById(id).className = 'imgborderon';
      }
     else if (document.layers)
    {
         for (var i=0; i < imgThumbArr.length; i++ )
         {
 	  if (document.imgThumbArr[i])
           {
             document.imgThumbArr[i].className = 'image';
 	  }
 	}
 	document.id.className = 'imgborderon';
    }
    else
   {
         for (var i=0; i < imgThumbArr.length; i++ )
         {
           if (document.all.imgThumbArr[i])
           {
 	    document.all.imgThumbArr[i].className = 'image';
           }
 	}
  	document.all.id.className = 'imgborderon';
   }
 }

   <script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
    //added by Sandip 3/2012 - 'processing' while item gets loaded into cart
     function ProcessingMsg(name) {
         document.getElementById(name).innerHTML = "Processing";
     }
 
 //added by Sandip 3/2012 - expandable text
     function toggle(displayText, toggleText) {
         var ele = document.getElementById(toggleText);
         var text = document.getElementById(displayText);
         if (ele.style.display == "block") {
             ele.style.display = "none";
             //text.innerHTML = "show";
         }
         else {
             ele.style.display = "block";
             //text.innerHTML = "hide";
         }
     }
   </script>

     var customSearchOptions = {};
     customSearchOptions['adoptions'] = {'layout': 'noTop'};
     var customSearchControl = new google.search.CustomSearchControl(
       '004057667419395696453:0a7-qdptpe4', customSearchOptions);
     customSearchControl.setResultSetSize(google.search.Search.SMALL_RESULTSET);
     var options = new google.search.DrawOptions();
     options.setAutoComplete(true);
     customSearchControl.draw('cse', options);
   }, true);

                <!-- Expandable description -->
                <tr>
                 <td style="padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 10px" valign="top">
                  <div align="justify">
                   <font color="#000000" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" size="2">
                    <strong>
                     Description
                    </strong>
                    <br/>
                    <div id="displayText3">
                     <!--        The 100% waterproof RoofBag Cross Country car top carrier offers the best weather protection and durability in the market. Heavy-duty material, coated on both sides with an abrasion-resistant vinyl layer, electrically sealed joints, waterproof fabric, waterproof zipper, zipper flap, water-repellent straps and no exposed stitching, allow it to withstand severe weather conditions and rough handling.<br> -->
                     The RoofBag Cross Country carrier is 100% waterproof and offers the best weather protection and durability in the market.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     No exposed stitching and 2-year warranty means peace of mind even for the longest trip in the most severe weather.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <!-- <a  href="javascript:toggle('displayText3','toggleText1'); " id="ToggleMore1"> Read More ...</a>												</div><br>
                                                  
                                              <div id="toggleText1" align="left" style="display: none">-->
                     <a class="showLink" href="#" id="example-show" onclick="showHide('example');return false;" style="color:#010101">
                      Click for More Details
                     </a>
                     <div class="more" id="example">
                      <br/>
                      <!--<ul>
 <li>Roof 58" or Longer: 11 Cubic Feet or 15 Cubic Feet</li>
 <li>Roof 40" to 58": 11 Cubic Feet</li>
 <li>Roof shorter than 40": Neither size fits</li>
 <li><a href="/Car-Top-Carriers-Sizing-Information.asp">What Size Fits My Car?</a></li> 
 </ul>-->
                      <b>
                       What size fits my car?
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Size 11
                      </b>
                      fits all vehicles - Same storage space as 4 medium-size suitcases.
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Size 15
                      </b>
                      fits full-size sedans, SUVs and vans - Equivalent to 5 medium-size suitcases.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Which straps should I choose?
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      Choose
                      <b>
                       Rack
                      </b>
                      if you have side rails, cross bars, or basket.
                      <br/>
                      Choose
                      <b>
                       No Rack
                      </b>
                      if you have a bare roof (no rack) or flush rails.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       How is it installed?
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       On side rails:
                      </b>
                      straps attach to side rails left-to-right.
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       On cross bars:
                      </b>
                      straps attach to bars front-to-back.
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       On bare roof (no rack):
                      </b>
                      straps pass through the inside of the car through door frame. Doors close over straps.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       What's Included?
                      </b>
                      <li>
                       RoofBag Cross Country Carrier
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Set of 2 Straps (When ordering, choose Rack
                       <b>
                        OR
                       </b>
                       No Rack)
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Installation Booklet
                      </li>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Optional Straps (Sold Separately)
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      Door Hook Straps provide an alternative way to secure the carrier to the door frame, avoiding the overhead strap.
                      <br/>
                      For these straps to fit, the top section of the door frame needs to have a vertical ridge about 1/2" wide x 1/2" high, sticking down from the frame.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Warranty
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      RoofBag Cross-Country car top carriers are covered with a 2-year warranty against defects in materials and workmanship.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Shipping
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      Ships the same day if order is placed on a business day (M-F) before 2:45PM PST.
                      <br/>
                      <a class="hideLink" href="#" id="example-hide" onclick="showHide('example');return false;">
                       Less Details
                      </a>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </font>

         <td height="50" colspan="4" valign="top" style="padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 10px">
 									 	<div align="justify">
                                       
 
                                       
                                       	<font color="#000000" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" size="2">
 										<strong><br>Description:</strong>
                                     
                                           <div id="Wrap2">
                                             The RoofBag Explorer car top 
 											  carrier offers excellent weather 
 											  protection at an economical price. 
 											  This car top carrier features 
 											  truly waterproof fabric (not just water 
 											  resistant or weatherproof), 
 											  waterproof zipper, 2" zipper flap, double-stitched corners, and water-repellent 1.5"-wide straps. The zipper flap is sewn instead of electrically sealed. This presents a potential for minor water wicking through the needle holes in heavy rain. However, we have never heard from anyone experiencing any water penetration in these very well designed and durable carriers with great water-proofness and an excellent price.											                <a href="#" id="example2-show" class="showLink" onclick="showHide('example2');return false;">More...</a>   <div id="example2" class="more">                                     
                                                                                    <br>
 
 <strong>Straps:</strong><br>Straps are unique in the market: heavy-duty, seat-belt type, 1.5 inches wide, 1,000-pounds strong. They are water-repellent to avoid water wicking into the car. Each strap includes two genuine YKK, super-tough delrin side-release buckles. They provide easy access to the roof top carrier's contents from either side of the carrier.<br><br>
 										  		   <strong>Construction:</strong><br>The material used in the Explorer car top carriers is made with 18-oz, heavy-duty tight-knit polyester fabric, coated on both sides with an abrasion-resistant vinyl layer. This means that our carriers can withstand the severe rigors of travel without cracking, peeling or ripping: extreme temperatures, constant beating by high-speed wind, and prolonged exposure to sun, rain, snow, sleet, sand or dust. The exclusive fabric formulation of the Explorer resists peeling like no other carrier in the market. <br><br>
 										  		   <strong>Versatile Design: </strong><br>RoofBag rooftop carriers are made to work with bare roof tops (no rack), cross bars, side rails and can also can be installed on cars with sunroof.<br><br>
 										  		   <strong>Warranty:</strong><br>All RoofBag carriers are covered with a 2-year warranty against defects in materials and workmanship.<br>
 <a href="#" id="example2-hide" class="hideLink" onclick="showHide('example2');return false;">Less Text</a>
                                           </div> 
                                           </div>
                                           </font>

 										  protects roof and keeps RoofBag 
 										  carrier from sliding.<br>
 									  
 									- Extra Straps -  to 
 										  fasten carrier in different ways.<br>
 
 									  
 									  
 								- Duffle Bags - help 
 										  pack, organize, load and unload the 
 										  RoofBag carrier.<br> 
 								- Tire   Step -  helps reach top of 
 										  car easily.<br>

                  <tr>
                   <td style="padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 10px" valign="top">
                    <div align="justify">
                     <font color="#000000" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" size="2">
                      <strong>
                       Description
                      </strong>
                      <br/>
                      <div id="Wrap2">
                       <!--        The 99% waterproof RoofBag Explorer Soft Car Top Carrier offers excellent weather protection at an economical price. Heavy-duty material, coated on both sides with an abrasion-resistant vinyl layer means that our carriers can withstand the severe rigors of travel without cracking, peeling or ripping, extreme temperatures, constant beating by high-speed wind, and prolonged exposure to sun, rain, snow, sleet, sand or dust.	     -->
                       The 99% waterproof RoofBag Explorer carrier offers excellent weather protection at an economical price and can withstand the severe rigors of travel.
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <a class="showLink" href="#" id="example2-show" onclick="showHide('example2');return false;" style="color:#010101">
                        Click for More Details
                       </a>
                       <div class="more" id="example2">
                        <!--<a  href="javascript:toggle('Div5','toggleText55'); " border=0 id="ToggleMore2"> 
 											More ...</a></div>
                                           <div id="toggleText55" align="left" style="display: none"> <br>-->
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         What size fits my car?
                        </b>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         Size 11
                        </b>
                        fits all vehicles - Same storage space as 4 medium-size suitcases.
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         Size 15
                        </b>
                        fits full-size sedans, SUVs and vans - Equivalent to 5 medium-size suitcases.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         Which straps should I choose?
                        </b>
                        <br/>
                        Choose
                        <b>
                         Rack
                        </b>
                        if you have side rails, cross bars, or basket.
                        <br/>
                        Choose
                        <b>
                         No Rack
                        </b>
                        if you have a bare roof (no rack) or flush rails.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         How is it installed?
                        </b>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         On side rails:
                        </b>
                        straps attach to side rails left-to-right.
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         On cross bars:
                        </b>
                        straps attach to bars front-to-back.
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         On bare roof (no rack):
                        </b>
                        straps pass through the inside of the car through door frame. Doors close over straps.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         What's Included?
                        </b>
                        <li>
                         RoofBag Explorer Carrier
                        </li>
                        <li>
                         Set of 2 Straps (When ordering, choose Rack
                         <b>
                          OR
                         </b>
                         No Rack)
                        </li>
                        <li>
                         Installation Booklet
                        </li>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         Optional Straps (Sold Separately)
                        </b>
                        <br/>
                        Door Hook Straps provide an alternative way to secure the carrier to the door frame, avoiding the overhead strap.
                        <br/>
                        For these straps to fit, the top section of the door frame needs to have a vertical ridge about 1/2" wide x 1/2" high, sticking down from the frame.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         Warranty
                        </b>
                        <br/>
                        RoofBag Explorer car top carriers are covered with a 1-year warranty against defects in materials and workmanship.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        <b>
                         Shipping
                        </b>
                        <br/>
                        Ships the same day if order is placed on a business day (M-F) before 2:45PM PST.
                        <br/>
                        <a class="hideLink" href="#" id="example2-hide" onclick="showHide('example2');return false;">
                         Less Details
                        </a>
                       </div>
                      </div>
                     </font>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="color:black; font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; text-align:left; font-size:12px">

                     <br/>
                     <div style="color:black; font-family:Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size:13px; text-align:justify">
                      <b>
                       What's the difference between Cross-Country and Explorer?
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Cross Country:
                      </b>
                      100% waterproof, all joints are electrically welded, 
 		guaranteed for 2 years.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Explorer:
                      </b>
                      99% waterproof, more economical because the zipper flap is stitched, guaranteed for 1 year.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       Both
                      </b>
                      car top carriers are the same size and shape, and use the same heavy-duty, waterproof fabric and the same waterproof zipper.
                      <br/>

                            <tr>
                             <td align="center" colspan="3" style="padding-left: 10px; padding-right: 10px" valign="top" width="520">
                              <div align="justify">
                               <font color="#000000" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" size="2">
                                <br/>
                                <b>
                                 Description
                                </b>
                                <br/>
                                A protective non-slip roof mat that prevents slipping or sliding of the carrier, increasing stability and safety. It also prevents scratches of the roof caused by dirt.
                                <a href="javascript:toggle('displayText3','toggleText17'); " id="ToggleMore17">
                                 <br/>
                                 <br/>
                                 <strong>
                                  Features
                                 </strong>
                                 <br/>
                                </a>
                                <br/>
                               </font>
                              </div>
                              <div align="left" id="toggleText17" style="display: none">
                               <font color="#000000" face="Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif" size="2">
                                <ul>
                                 <li>
                                  Provides extra padding and protects the roof paint during travel.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Strongly recommended for cars without a roof rack.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Also recommended for cars with a roof rack.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Adds friction between carrier and roof, preventing slipping or sliding.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Made of special non-slip, rubbery webbing material, 5/32" thick.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Mildew and UV resistant for durability.
                                 </li>
                                 <li>
                                  Color: Dark Gray
                                 </li>
                                </ul>
                               </font>
                              </div>
                             </td>

                            Each RoofBag carrier "For Cars Without Rack" comes with 2 Pass-Through straps that work on cars without rack. Order an extra set of Pass-Through Straps if you have a large van or SUV without rack, so that you can splice straps together to make extra-long straps. Also on a SUV or a 2-door car with a rear gate, extra-long straps allow running the straps through the rear gate. On cars with a curved roof, an extra pass-through strap holding down the front of the carrier will keep the front of the bag from lifting up during travel, for a more quiet ride.
                            <br/>
                            <br/>
                           </font>
                          </td>
                         </tr>
                        </table>
                       </td>

For these straps to fit, the top section of door frame needs to have a vertical ridge about 1/2" wide x 1/2" high, sticking down from the frame.

 		function UpdateLiveCard(){

 			var regexCAZip	=/(^[A-Za-z]\d[A-Za-z](\s{0,1})\d[A-Za-z]\d$)/;
 			var regexENZip  =/(^(([gG][iI][rR] {0,}0[aA]{2})|((([a-pr-uwyzA-PR-UWYZ][a-hk-yA-HK-Y]?[0-9][0-9]?)|(([a-pr-uwyzA-PR-UWYZ][0-9][a-hjkstuwA-HJKSTUW])|([a-pr-uwyzA-PR-UWYZ][a-hk-yA-HK-Y][0-9][abehmnprv-yABEHMNPRV-Y]))) {0,}[0-9][abd-hjlnp-uw-zABD-HJLNP-UW-Z]{2}))$)/;

 //adding value to lcZip.value allowed this if statement to execute, even with first zip digit
 //next if executes only if a new zip code is being written and there was no previous zip code (PreZip) or the new zip code is different
 				if (lcZip.value.length != 0 && (lcPreZip.value.replace(/ /,"") != lcZip.value.replace(/ /,"") || lcPreZip.value.length == 0 )){

 //works: executes only after full zip or postal code (but doesn't execute in GS test page)	
 						if (regexUSZip.test(lcZip.value) == true){
 							shippinglocCountry.value = "US";							
 						}
 //						else {							
 						else if (regexCAZip.test(lcZip.value) == true){							
 							shippinglocCountry.value = "CA";	
 						}
 						else {							
 							shippinglocCountry.value = "EN";

 //works: US or CA or EN 
 						lcAction.value = "getshiprates";
 						var getingShipInfo =  document.getElementById("getingShipInfo");
 						getingShipInfo.style.display = "inline";											
 						lcFormLiveCart.submit();
 					}
 				}
 			}
 		}

  					&&(  (state.value.length == 0 && country.value != "US" && country.value != "CA" && country.value != "EN") ||
 //					     (   (state.options[state.selectedIndex].text.indexOf("(CA)") != -1 && country.value == "CA" && regexCAZip.test(zip.value)) ||
  //					 	     (state.options[state.selectedIndex].text.indexOf("(US)") != -1 && country.value == "US" && regexUSZip.test(zip.value))
  // JC 5.7.2012: correct errors in previous two lines: == true was missing - may need to correct "state" to "country" in next line
 					     (   (state.options[state.selectedIndex].text.indexOf("(CA)") != -1 && country.value == "CA" && regexCAZip.test(zip.value) == true) ||
 					 	     (state.options[state.selectedIndex].text.indexOf("(US)") != -1 && country.value == "US" && regexUSZip.test(zip.value) == true) ||
 					 	     (state.options[state.selectedIndex].text.indexOf("(EN)") != -1 && country.value == "EN" && regexENZip.test(zip.value) == true) 				 	     
 					     )
 					  )
 				    )
 				{
 
 // test4					
 //			document.cookie="test4" + "=" +escape(country.value)+ " " +escape(zip)+ " " +escape(state)+ ""
 					
 					
 					if (preShipState.value != state.value || preShipZip.value != zip.value || preShipCountry.value != country.value )
 					{
 
 // test5
 //			document.cookie="test5" + "=" +escape(country.value)+ " " +escape(zip)+ " " +escape(state)+ ""
 
 						action.value = "updateShipInfo";
 						preShipState.value = state.value;
 						preShipZip.value = zip.value;
 						preShipCountry.value = country.value;
 						updateMsg.innerHTML = "Getting Shipping Info";
 						shippingInfo.submit();
 
 // test6
 //			document.cookie="test6" + "=" +escape(country.value)+ " " +escape(zip)+ " " +escape(state)+ ""
 
 					}
 				}
 			}
 }
 
 
 function saveQCIParam(paramName,value)
 {
 			var mainStr;
 			var aidOrder,aName,aLastName,aPhone,aAddress,aCity,aZip,alocState,alocCountry,ashippingName,ashippingLastName,ashippingPhone,ashippingAddress,ashippingCity,ashippingZip,ashippingLocState,ashippingLocCountry, adiscCode,aidCust;
 			aidOrder=aName=aLastName=aPhone=aAddress=aCity=aZip=alocState=alocCountry=ashippingName=ashippingLastName=ashippingPhone=ashippingAddress=ashippingCity=ashippingZip=ashippingLocState=ashippingLocCountry= adiscCode=aidCust="";
 			mainStr = getCookie("QuickCustomerInfo");
 			if (mainStr.length > 0)
 			{
 				mainStr = mainStr.split("*|*");
 				try{
 					aidOrder		= mainStr[0]+"";
 					aName			= mainStr[1]+"";
 					aLastName		= mainStr[2]+"";
 					aPhone			= mainStr[3]+"";
 					aAddress		= mainStr[4]+"";
 					aCity			= mainStr[5]+"";
 					aZip			= mainStr[6]+"";
 					alocState		= mainStr[7]+"";
 					alocCountry		= mainStr[8]+"";
 					ashippingName	= mainStr[9]+"";
 					ashippingLastName= mainStr[10]+"";
 					ashippingPhone	= mainStr[11]+"";
 					ashippingAddress= mainStr[12]+"";
 					ashippingCity	= mainStr[13]+"";
 					ashippingZip	= mainStr[14]+"";
 					ashippingLocState= mainStr[15]+"";
 					ashippingLocCountry= mainStr[16]+"";
 					adiscCode		= mainStr[17]+"";
 					aidCust			= mainStr[18]+"";
 				}
 				catch(E){ }
 			}			
 			
 			try{ eval("a"+paramName+"=value"); }
 			catch(E){}
 
 			mainStr = aidOrder + "*|*" + aName + "*|*" + aLastName + "*|*"  + aPhone + "*|*" + aAddress + "*|*" + aCity	+ "*|*" + aZip + "*|*"+ alocState + "*|*" + alocCountry + "*|*" + ashippingName + "*|*" + ashippingLastName	+ "*|*" + ashippingPhone	+ "*|*" + ashippingAddress + "*|*" + ashippingCity + "*|*" + ashippingZip + "*|*" + ashippingLocState + "*|*" + ashippingLocCountry + "*|*"  + adiscCode	+ "*|*" + aidCust;
 			setCookie("QuickCustomerInfo", mainStr);
 }
